## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram
    [*] --> UP
    UP --> DOWN : start / pointerdown
    DOWN --> UP : end / pointerup
    UP --> UP : setDisabled / setState(UP)
    DOWN --> DOWN : setDisabled / setState(DOWN)
```
